### [147] [Locality for Codes over the Integers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26756)
*Giulia Cavicchioni,Eleonora Guerrini,Julien Lavauzelle*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究整数环上的局部可恢复码，提出加权局部性概念、给出类 Singleton 界，并构造若干满足局部性的码，包括 Tamo–Barg 码的整数类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统局部可恢复码多在有限域上研究，而实际存储或代数编码场景可能涉及乘积整数剩余环。作者希望将局部性理论推广到 \(\mathbb{Z}/q_1\mathbb{Z} \times \cdots \times \mathbb{Z}/q_n\mathbb{Z}\)，并建立相应的距离界与构造方法。

Method: 引入适用于不同模数坐标的加权局部性定义；在该框架下分析码的参数关系，推导类 Singleton 上界；进一步设计具有局部恢复性质的整数环码构造，并给出 Tamo–Barg 型构造的整数版本。

Result: 论文得到整数乘积环上局部可恢复码的 Singleton-like bound，并提出多种达到或接近该界的构造思路，表明有限域 LRC 的若干核心结构可推广到整数模环环境。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了局部可恢复码理论的代数基础，为非有限域/整数模环上的分布式存储编码提供了参数界与构造工具。

Abstract: In this work, we study the codes over the integers with locality constraints. We introduce a weighted notion of locality over $\mathbb{Z}/q_1\mathbb{Z} \times \cdots \times \mathbb{Z}/q_n\mathbb{Z}$ and derive a Singleton-like bound for locally recoverable codes. We also propose some code constructions with locality, including integer analogs of Tamo--Barg codes.

</details>


### [148] [Input Distribution Design for Ranging-Oriented OFDM-ISAC Systems Under Frequency-Selective Fading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26778)
*Weijiang Zhao,Yifeng Xiong*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究6G OFDM-ISAC系统中的输入分布/星座设计，提出一种计算高效的方法，在频率选择性信道下平衡通信速率与感知性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OFDM-ISAC系统需要同时满足通信与感知目标，而星座设计会直接影响通信容量和感知失真；现有方法需要在实际感知约束下实现有效权衡。

Method: 基于容量-失真理论框架，将星座峰度视为可分配资源，并在不同子载波上进行合理分配，以适应频率选择性信道和实际感知约束。

Result: 提出的方法能够以较高计算效率完成输入分布设计，并揭示在实际感知约束下，跨子载波分配星座峰度是优化通信-感知权衡的关键策略。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，OFDM-ISAC中的星座峰度管理可作为一种核心设计原则，有助于在6G场景下实现通信速率与感知性能之间的良好平衡。

Abstract: The implementation of the \ac{isac} feature in \ac{6g} networks is most likely to be based on the framework of \ac{ofdm}. Input distribution design, or constellation design, is a crucial technique in \ac{ofdm}-\ac{isac} systems enabling a favorable balance between communication rate and sensing performance. In this treatise, we propose a computationally efficient input distribution design approach for \ac{ofdm}-\ac{isac} under frequency-selective channels, following the theoretical framework of capacity distortion. We highlight that under practical sensing constraints, the optimal strategy is to treat the kurtosis of constellations as a resource, and allocate it appropriately over subcarriers.

</details>


### [149] [Joint Transceiver Orientation Optimization for Rotatable-Antenna MIMO Capacity Maximization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26845)
*Zheng Ailing,Wu Qingqing,Peng Xingxiang,Peng Qiaoyan,Zheng Ziyuan,Chen Wen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究可旋转天线辅助的 MIMO 通信，通过联合优化发射协方差矩阵与收发端天线朝向，在实际球冠约束下提升信道容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 MIMO 通常使用固定天线阵列，难以根据传播环境自适应重构有效信道矩阵；可旋转天线提供了朝向域自由度，有望进一步提升容量。

Method: 建立朝向相关的 MIMO 信道模型；将容量最大化表述为联合优化发射协方差矩阵和收发端可旋转天线朝向的非凸问题；采用交替优化框架，其中发射协方差通过特征模传输与注水法更新，天线朝向通过黎曼 Frank-Wolfe 方法优化；并分析低信噪比下的 MISO/SIMO 特例简化设计。

Result: 数值结果表明，所提出的可旋转天线辅助 MIMO 设计相比固定朝向基准可显著提升信道容量。

Conclusion: 引入天线朝向域可重构能力能够有效改善 MIMO 信道条件并提升容量，可旋转天线为下一代自适应通信系统提供了有价值的新自由度。

Abstract: Conventional multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) systems mainly rely on fixed antenna arrays, which limits their capability to adapt the effective channel matrix to the propagation environment. Rotatable antennas (RAs), which enable mechanical or electronic adjustment of antenna boresight directions, introduce a new orientation-domain degree of freedom for channel reconfiguration. In this paper, we investigate an RA-aided MIMO communication system for channel capacity enhancement. We first establish an orientation-dependent MIMO channel model. Then, we formulate a capacity maximization problem by jointly optimizing the transmit covariance matrix and the transmit/receive RA orientations under practical spherical-cap constraints. To solve this non-convex problem, we develop an alternating optimization algorithm, where the transmit covariance matrix is updated via eigenmode transmission and water-filling, while each RA orientation is optimized through a Riemannian Frank-Wolfe method. We further investigate the low-SNR regime and derive simplified designs for multiple-input single-output (MISO) and single-input multiple-output (SIMO) special cases. Numerical results show that the proposed RA-aided MIMO design significantly improves the channel capacity compared with the fixed-orientation benchmark, demonstrating the benefits of orientation-domain channel reconfiguration.

</details>
